## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the canonical form of population dynamics ODEs. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying carrying capacity.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Logistic with Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (strong Allee effect with minimum viable population)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism vs catabolism power-law balance)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Time-dependent Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponential growth with time-varying rate)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth with proportional harvesting)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant yield harvesting)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (generalized density-dependent growth)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent birth with linear death)
- Time-modulated logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal variation in growth)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear dependence on P (dP/dt ∝ P) → exponential/Malthusian regime indicating density-independent growth
- Quadratic terms in P (dP/dt contains P² term) → logistic-type density dependence with self-limiting competition
- Cubic terms in P (dP/dt contains P³ term) → Allee effect or bistability with critical population thresholds
- Logarithmic dependence log(P) → Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically
- Ratio P/(1+cP) structure → Beverton-Holt or Michaelis-Menten type saturating reproduction
- Difference of power laws (P^a - P^b) → competing metabolic scaling processes (anabolism vs catabolism)
- Constant additive/subtractive term independent of P → external forcing such as immigration, harvesting, or stocking
- Explicit time dependence with periodic functions → seasonal or cyclic environmental forcing on growth parameters
- Product of multiple linear factors in P → multiple equilibria and critical population thresholds in the dynamics
